##-----------------TITLE------------------------##
Hot Shots vs Red Hot Chili Peppers
##------------------TEXT------------------------##
Prev: Major PainUp: Hot ShotsNext: Spunkee MonkeysHot Shots vs Red Hot Chili Peppers
The game ended on a sour note as the ump tried to deny the Hot Shots their last at-bat,
then with the tieing run at bat called her out on a strike that bounced in the dirt in front of the catcher's feet.  Score 6-3.  I got very few photos due to a combination of factors:
messy backgrounds at the Heritage field, big shadows across most of the infield, few close plays, feeling that I already had plenty of easy set shots of players in batting stance etc from other games, and photographer error (out of position for Breanna's home run).

Hot Shots vs Spunkee Monkeys
##------------------TEXT------------------------##

The Hot Shots finally came out of their slump, cruising to an 8-1 victory.
Jennifer played a key role, pitching two innings of relief and giving up only
a solo homer despite her wind-up-free style.  My shooting came out of a slump, too -- I don't know why
so many of the photos ended up vertical, though.
